openvdb-devel in Fedora 32

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of openvdb-devel. You might want go back to the main page of openvdb-devel.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-01-29 Fedora Release Engineering - 7.0.0-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2019-12-11 Luya Tshimbalanga - 7.0.0-1 - Update to 7.0.0 - Set python3 module installation path via cmake - Drop epydoc dependency
2019-09-19 Luya Tshimbalanga - 6.2.0-1 - Update to 6.2.0 - Drop no longer needed upstream patch - Rename subpackge module to python3-* - Fix correct python module installation path

2019-07-25 Fedora Release Engineering - 6.0.0-3 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_31_Mass_Rebuild
